    <path d="M8 0a8 8 0 1 1 0 16A8 8 0 0 1 8 0ZM1.5 8a6.5 6.5 0 1 0 13 0 6.5 6.5 0 0 0-13 0Zm4.879-2.773 4.264 2.559a.25.25 0 0 1 0 .428l-4.264 2.559A.25.25 0 0 1 6 10.559V5.442a.25.25 0 0 1 .379-.215Z"></path>
</svg>
        </span>

        <span data-view-component="true" class="ActionListItem-label">
          Actions
</span>      
</a>

</li>
        <li hidden="hidden" data-menu-item="i5projects-tab" data-targets="action-list.items" role="none" data-view-component="true" class="ActionListItem">


    <a tabindex="-1" id="item-76bd194e-3caa-4cfb-9446-511298db9e7e" href="/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/projects" role="menuitem" data-view-component="true" class="ActionListContent ActionListContent--visual16">
        <span class="ActionListItem-visual ActionListItem-visual--leading">
          <svg aria-hidden="true" height="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" data-view-component="true" class="octicon octicon-table">
    <path d="M0 1.75C0 .784.784 0 1.75 0h12.5C15.216 0 16 .784 16 1.75v12.5A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.25 16H1.75A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 0 14.25ZM6.5 6.5v8h7.75a.25.25 0 0 0 .25-.25V6.5Zm8-1.5V1.75a.25.25 0 0 0-.25-.25H6.5V5Zm-13 1.5v7.75c0 .138.112.25.25.25H5v-8ZM5 5V1.5H1.75a.25.25 0 0 0-.25.25V5Z"></path>

        </span>

          Projects

                <div class="markdown-heading"><h1 class="heading-element">AdGuard Home - FAQ</h1><a id="user-content-adguard-home---faq" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: AdGuard Home - FAQ" href="#adguard-home---faq"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This article is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>

<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#doesntblock" id="user-content-doesntblock" name="user-content-doesntblock">Why AdGuard Home doesn't block ads?</a></h2><a id="user-content-why-adguard-home-doesnt-block-ads" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why AdGuard Home doesn't block ads?" href="#why-adguard-home-doesnt-block-ads"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#doesntblock" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>Suppose that AdGuard Home must block <code>somebadsite.com</code> but for some reason it
doesn't.  Let's try to resolve this issue.</p>
<p>Most likely you didn't configure your device to use AdGuard Home as its default
DNS server.  To check if you're using AdGuard Home as the default DNS server:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>On Windows, open a Terminal window (Start → Run → <code>cmd.exe</code>).  On other
systems, open your Terminal application.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Execute <code>nslookup example.org</code>.  It will print something like this:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="Server:         192.168.0.1
Address:        192.168.0.1#53

Non-authoritative answer:
Name:   example.org
Address: &lt;IPv4&gt;
Name:   example.org
Address: &lt;IPv6&gt;"><pre lang="none" class="notranslate"><code>Server:         192.168.0.1
Address:        192.168.0.1#53

Non-authoritative answer:
Name:   example.org
Address: &lt;IPv4&gt;
Name:   example.org
Address: &lt;IPv6&gt;
</code></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Check if the <code>Server</code> IP address is the one on which AdGuard Home is
running.  If not, you need to configure your device, see
<a href="#defaultdns">below</a>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Ensure that your request to <code>example.org</code> appears in the AdGuard Home UI on
the Query Log page.  If not, you need to configure AdGuard Home to listen on
the specified network interface.  The most straightforward way to do so is
to reinstall AdGuard Home with default settings.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<p>If you are sure that your device uses AdGuard Home as its default DNS server,
but the problem persists, it might have something to do with an AdGuard Home
misconfiguration.  Please check and ensure that:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>You have the “Block domains using filters and hosts files” setting enabled
on the “Settings → General settings” page.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>You have the appropriate safety mechanisms, such as Parental Control,
enabled on the “Settings → General settings”.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>You have the appropriate filters enabled on the “Filters → DNS blocklists”
page.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>You don't have any exception rule lists that may allow the requests enabled
on the “Filters → DNS allowlists” page.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>You don't have any DNS rewrites that may interfere with the “Filters → DNS
rewrites” page.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>You don't have any custom filtering rules that may interfere with the
“Filters → Custom filtering rules” page.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#logs" id="user-content-logs" name="user-content-logs">Where can I inspect the logs?</a></h2><a id="user-content-where-can-i-inspect-the-logs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Where can I inspect the logs?" href="#where-can-i-inspect-the-logs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#logs" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>The default location of the plain-text logs (not to be confused with the query
logs) depends on the operating system and installation mode:</p>

<ul>
<li>
<p><strong>OpenWrt Linux:</strong> use the <code>logread -e AdGuardHome</code> command.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Linux</strong> systems with <strong>systemd</strong> and other <strong>Unix</strong> systems with
<strong>SysV-style init:</strong> <code>/var/log/AdGuardHome.err</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>macOS:</strong> <code>/var/log/AdGuardHome.stderr.log</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>Linux</strong> systems with <strong>Snapcraft</strong> use the <code>snap logs adguard-home</code>
command.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>FreeBSD:</strong> <code>/var/log/daemon.log</code> (<strong>since v0.108.0-b.4</strong>).  Before
<strong>v0.108.0-b.4</strong> no logs are written by default.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><strong>OpenBSD:</strong> <code>/var/log/daemon</code> (<strong>since v0.108.0-b.4</strong>).  Before
<strong>v0.108.0-b.4</strong> no logs are written by default.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>On <strong>Windows:</strong> the <a href="https://docs.microsoft.com/en-us/windows/win32/wes/windows-event-log" rel="nofollow">Windows Event Log</a> is used.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#verboselog" id="user-content-verboselog" name="user-content-verboselog">How to configure AdGuard Home to write verbose-level logs?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-configure-adguard-home-to-write-verbose-level-logs" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to configure AdGuard Home to write verbose-level logs?" href="#how-to-configure-adguard-home-to-write-verbose-level-logs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#verboselog" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>To troubleshoot a complicated issue, the verbose-level logging is sometimes
required.  Here's how to enable it:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Stop AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./AdGuardHome -s stop"><pre>./AdGuardHome -s stop</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Configure AdGuard Home to write verbose-level logs:</p>
<ol>
<li>Open <code>AdGuardHome.yaml</code> in your editor.</li>
<li>Set <code>log.file</code> to the desired path of the log file, for example
<code>/tmp/aghlog.txt</code>.  Note that the directory must exist.</li>
<li>Set <code>log.verbose</code> to <code>true</code>.</li>
</ol>
<p><strong>NOTE:</strong> Before v0.107.34 use <code>verbose</code> and <code>log_file</code> properties.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Restart AdGuard Home and reproduce the issue:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./AdGuardHome -s start"><pre>./AdGuardHome -s start</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>

<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#customblock" id="user-content-customblock" name="user-content-customblock"><span name="user-content-pixelsrv"></span>How to show a custom block page?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-show-a-custom-block-page" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to show a custom block page?" href="#how-to-show-a-custom-block-page"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#customblock" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">A note about HTTPS</h3><a id="user-content-a-note-about-https" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: A note about HTTPS" href="#a-note-about-https"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>Before doing any of this, please note that modern browsers are set up to use
HTTPS, so they validate the authenticity of the web server certificate.  That
means that using any of these will result in warning screens.</p>
<p>There are a couple of proposed extensions that, when they become reasonably well
supported by clients, would allow for a better user experience, including the
<a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/rfc8914" rel="nofollow">RFC 8914 Extended DNS Error codes</a> and the <a href="https://datatracker.ietf.org/doc/html/draft-reddy-dnsop-error-page-08" rel="nofollow">DNS Access Denied Error
Page RFC draft</a>.  We'll implement them when browsers actually start
to support them.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Prerequisites</h3><a id="user-content-prerequisites" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Prerequisites" href="#prerequisites"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>To use any of these ways to show a custom block page, you'll need an HTTP server
running on some IP address and serving the page in question on all routes.
Something like <a href="https://github.com/kvic-z/pixelserv-tls"><code>pixelserv-tls</code></a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Custom block page for Parental Control and Safe Browsing filters</h3><a id="user-content-custom-block-page-for-parental-control-and-safe-browsing-filters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Custom block page for Parental Control and Safe Browsing filters" href="#custom-block-page-for-parental-control-and-safe-browsing-filters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>There is currently no way to set these parameters from the UI, so you'll need to
edit the configuration file manually:</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Stop AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./AdGuardHome -s stop"><pre>./AdGuardHome -s stop</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Open <code>AdGuardHome.yaml</code> in your editor.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Set the <code>dns.parental_block_host</code> or <code>dns.safebrowsing_block_host</code> settings
to the IP address of the server (in this example, <code>192.168.123.45</code>):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-yaml notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# …
dns:
  # …

  # NOTE: Change to the actual IP address of your server.
  parental_block_host: 192.168.123.45
  safebrowsing_block_host: 192.168.123.45"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> …</span>
<span class="pl-ent">dns</span>:
  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> …</span>

  <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> NOTE: Change to the actual IP address of your server.</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">parental_block_host</span>: <span class="pl-s">192.168.123.45</span>
  <span class="pl-ent">safebrowsing_block_host</span>: <span class="pl-s">192.168.123.45</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Restart AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./AdGuardHome -s start"><pre>./AdGuardHome -s start</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Custom block page for other filters</h3><a id="user-content-custom-block-page-for-other-filters" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Custom block page for other filters" href="#custom-block-page-for-other-filters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Open the web UI.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Open the “Settings → DNS settings” page.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>In the “DNS server configuration” section, select the “Custom IP” radio
button in the “Blocking mode” selector and enter the IPv4 and IPv6 addresses
of the server.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Click “Save”.</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#webaddr" id="user-content-webaddr" name="user-content-webaddr">How to change dashboard interface's address?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-change-dashboard-interfaces-address" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to change dashboard interface's address?" href="#how-to-change-dashboard-interfaces-address"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#webaddr" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Stop AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./AdGuardHome -s stop"><pre>./AdGuardHome -s stop</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Open <code>AdGuardHome.yaml</code> in your editor.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Set the <code>http.address</code> setting to a new network interface.  For example:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p><code>0.0.0.0:0</code> to listen on all network interfaces.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>0.0.0.0:8080</code> to listen on all network interfaces with port <code>8080</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p><code>127.0.0.1:0</code> to listen on the local loopback interface only.</p>
</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>
<p>Restart AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="./AdGuardHome -s start"><pre>./AdGuardHome -s start</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#defaultdns" id="user-content-defaultdns" name="user-content-defaultdns">How to set up AdGuard Home as default DNS server?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-set-up-adguard-home-as-default-dns-server" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to set up AdGuard Home as default DNS server?" href="#how-to-set-up-adguard-home-as-default-dns-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/getting-started/#configure-devices" rel="nofollow">“Configuring Devices” section</a> on the “Getting Started” page in
the Knowledge Base.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#limitations" id="user-content-limitations" name="user-content-limitations">Are there any known limitations?</a></h2><a id="user-content-are-there-any-known-limitations" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Are there any known limitations?" href="#are-there-any-known-limitations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#limitations" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>Here are some examples of what cannot be blocked by a DNS-level blocker:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>YouTube, Twitch ads.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Facebook, Twitter, Instagram sponsored posts.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p>Essentially, any advertising that shares a domain with content cannot be blocked
by a DNS-level blocker.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Is there a chance to handle this in the future?</h3><a id="user-content-is-there-a-chance-to-handle-this-in-the-future" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Is there a chance to handle this in the future?" href="#is-there-a-chance-to-handle-this-in-the-future"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>DNS will never be enough to do this.  Your only option is to use a content
blocking proxy like what we do in the standalone AdGuard applications.  We're
going to bring this feature support to AdGuard Home in the future.
Unfortunately, even in this case, there still will be cases when this won't be
enough or would require quite complicated configuration.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#bindinuse" id="user-content-bindinuse" name="user-content-bindinuse">Why am I getting <code>bind: address already in use</code> error when trying to install on Ubuntu?</a></h2><a id="user-content-why-am-i-getting-bind-address-already-in-use-error-when-trying-to-install-on-ubuntu" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Why am I getting bind: address already in use error when trying to install on Ubuntu?" href="#why-am-i-getting-bind-address-already-in-use-error-when-trying-to-install-on-ubuntu"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#bindinuse" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>This happens because the port 53 on <code>localhost</code>, which is used for DNS, is
already taken by another program.  Ubuntu comes with a local DNS called
<code>systemd-resolved</code>, which uses the address <code>127.0.0.53:53</code> and thus prevents
AdGuard Home from binding to <code>127.0.0.1:53</code>.  You can see that by running:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo lsof -i :53"><pre>sudo lsof -i :53</pre></div>
<p>The output should be similar to:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="COMMAND     PID            USER   FD   TYPE DEVICE SIZE/OFF NODE NAME
systemd-r 14542 systemd-resolve   13u  IPv4  86178      0t0  UDP 127.0.0.53:domain
systemd-r 14542 systemd-resolve   14u  IPv4  86179      0t0  TCP 127.0.0.53:domain"><pre lang="none" class="notranslate"><code>COMMAND     PID            USER   FD   TYPE DEVICE SIZE/OFF NODE NAME
systemd-r 14542 systemd-resolve   13u  IPv4  86178      0t0  UDP 127.0.0.53:domain
systemd-r 14542 systemd-resolve   14u  IPv4  86179      0t0  TCP 127.0.0.53:domain
</code></pre></div>
<p>To fix this, you need to either disable the <code>systemd-resolved</code> daemon or choose
a different network interface and bind to an accessible IP address on it, for
instance, the IP address of your router inside your network.  But if you do need
to listen on <code>localhost</code>, there are several solutions.</p>
<p>Firstly, AdGuard Home can detect such configurations and disable
<code>systemd-resolved</code> for you if you press the “Fix” button, which is shown near
the <code>address already in use</code> message on the installation screen.</p>
<p>Secondly, if that doesn't work, follow the guide below.  Note that if you're
using AdGuard Home with docker or snap, you'll have to do it yourself.</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Create the <code>/etc/systemd/resolved.conf.d</code> directory, if necessary:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo mkdir -p /etc/systemd/resolved.conf.d"><pre>sudo mkdir -p /etc/systemd/resolved.conf.d</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Deactivate <code>DNSStubListener</code> and update DNS server address.  To do that,
create a new file, <code>/etc/systemd/resolved.conf.d/adguardhome.conf</code>, with the
following content:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-desktop notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="[Resolve]
DNS=127.0.0.1
DNSStubListener=no"><pre><span class="pl-en">[Resolve]</span>
<span class="pl-k">DNS</span>=127.0.0.1
<span class="pl-k">DNSStubListener</span>=no</pre></div>
<p>Specifying <code>127.0.0.1</code> as DNS server address <strong>is necessary</strong> because
otherwise the nameserver will be <code>127.0.0.53</code> which doesn't work without
<code>DNSStubListener</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Activate another <code>resolv.conf</code> file:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo mv /etc/resolv.conf /etc/resolv.conf.backup
sudo ln -s /run/systemd/resolve/resolv.conf /etc/resolv.conf"><pre>sudo mv /etc/resolv.conf /etc/resolv.conf.backup
sudo ln -s /run/systemd/resolve/resolv.conf /etc/resolv.conf</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Restart <code>DNSStubListener</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo systemctl reload-or-restart systemd-resolved"><pre>sudo systemctl reload-or-restart systemd-resolved</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<p>After that, <code>systemd-resolved</code> shouldn't be shown in the output of <code>lsof</code>, and
AdGuard Home should be able to bind to <code>127.0.0.1:53</code>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#reverseproxy" id="user-content-reverseproxy" name="user-content-reverseproxy">How to configure a reverse proxy server for AdGuard Home?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-configure-a-reverse-proxy-server-for-adguard-home" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to configure a reverse proxy server for AdGuard Home?" href="#how-to-configure-a-reverse-proxy-server-for-adguard-home"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#reverseproxy" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>If you're already running a web server and want to access the AdGuard Home
dashboard UI from a URL like <code>http://YOUR_SERVER/aghome/</code>, you can use this
configuration for your web server:</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">nginx</h3><a id="user-content-nginx" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: nginx" href="#nginx"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-nginx notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="location /aghome/ {
    proxy_cookie_path / /aghome/;
    proxy_pass http://AGH_IP:AGH_PORT/;
    proxy_redirect / /aghome/;
    proxy_set_header Host $host;
}"><pre><span class="pl-c1">location</span> /aghome/ <span class="pl-c1">{</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">proxy_cookie_path</span> / /aghome/<span class="pl-c1">;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">proxy_pass</span> <span class="pl-c1">http</span>://AGH_IP:AGH_PORT/<span class="pl-c1">;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">proxy_redirect</span> / /aghome/<span class="pl-c1">;</span>
    <span class="pl-c1">proxy_set_header</span> Host <span class="pl-v">$host</span><span class="pl-c1">;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">}</span></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">caddy</h3><a id="user-content-caddy" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: caddy" href="#caddy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=":80/aghome/* {
    route {
        uri strip_prefix /aghome
        reverse_proxy AGH_IP:AGH_PORT
    }
}"><pre lang="none" class="notranslate"><code>:80/aghome/* {
    route {
        uri strip_prefix /aghome
        reverse_proxy AGH_IP:AGH_PORT
    }
}
</code></pre></div>
<p>Or, if you just want to serve AdGuard Home with automatic TLS, use a
configuration similar to the example shown below:</p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="DOMAIN {
    encode gzip zstd
    tls YOUR_EMAIL@DOMAIN
    reverse_proxy AGH_IP:AGH_PORT
}"><pre lang="none" class="notranslate"><code>DOMAIN {
    encode gzip zstd
    tls YOUR_EMAIL@DOMAIN
    reverse_proxy AGH_IP:AGH_PORT
}
</code></pre></div>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Disable DoH encryption on AdGuard Home</h3><a id="user-content-disable-doh-encryption-on-adguard-home" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Disable DoH encryption on AdGuard Home" href="#disable-doh-encryption-on-adguard-home"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>When you use TLS on your reverse proxy server, there's no need to use TLS on
AdGuard Home.  Set <code>allow_unencrypted_doh: true</code> in <code>AdGuardHome.yaml</code> to allow
AdGuard Home respond to DoH requests without TLS encryption.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Real IP addresses of clients</h3><a id="user-content-real-ip-addresses-of-clients" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Real IP addresses of clients" href="#real-ip-addresses-of-clients"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p><strong>Since v0.107.0,</strong> you can set the parameter <code>trusted_proxies</code> to the IP
address(es) of your HTTP proxy to make AdGuard Home take the headers containing
the real client IP address into account.  See the <a href="https://github.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/wiki/Configuration">configuration</a> and
<a href="https://github.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/wiki/Encryption#reverse-proxy">encryption</a> pages for more information.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#fedora" id="user-content-fedora" name="user-content-fedora">How to fix <code>permission denied</code> errors on Fedora?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-fix-permission-denied-errors-on-fedora" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to fix permission denied errors on Fedora?" href="#how-to-fix-permission-denied-errors-on-fedora"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#fedora" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Move the <code>AdGuardHome</code> binary to <code>/usr/local/bin</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>As <code>root</code>, execute the following command to change the security context of
the file:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="chcon -t bin_t /usr/local/bin/AdGuardHome"><pre>chcon -t bin_t /usr/local/bin/AdGuardHome</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Add the required firewall rules in order to make it reachable through the
network.  For example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="firewall-cmd --new-zone=adguard --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-source=192.168.0.14/24 --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-port=3000/tcp --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-port=53/udp --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-port=80/tcp --permanent
firewall-cmd --reload"><pre>firewall-cmd --new-zone=adguard --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-source=192.168.0.14/24 --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-port=3000/tcp --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-port=53/udp --permanent
firewall-cmd --zone=adguard --add-port=80/tcp --permanent
firewall-cmd --reload</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<p>If you are still getting <code>code=exited status=203/EXEC</code> or similar errors from
<code>systemctl</code>, try uninstalling AdGuard Home and installing <em>directly</em> into
<code>/usr/local/bin</code> by using the <code>-o</code> option of the install script:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -s -S -L 'https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/master/scripts/install.sh' | sh -s -- -o '/usr/local/bin' -v"><pre>curl -s -S -L <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://raw.githubusercontent.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/master/scripts/install.sh<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> sh -s -- -o <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/usr/local/bin<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -v</pre></div>
<p>See <a href="https://github.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/issues/765#issuecomment-752262353">issue 765</a> and <a href="https://github.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/issues/3281">issue 3281</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#incompatfs" id="user-content-incompatfs" name="user-content-incompatfs">How to fix <code>incompatible file system</code> errors?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-fix-incompatible-file-system-errors" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to fix incompatible file system errors?" href="#how-to-fix-incompatible-file-system-errors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#incompatfs" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>You should move your AdGuard Home installation or working directory to another
location.  See the <a href="Getting-Started#limitations">limitations section</a> on the
“Getting Started” page.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#manual-update" id="user-content-manual-update" name="user-content-manual-update">How to update AdGuard Home manually?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-update-adguard-home-manually" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to update AdGuard Home manually?" href="#how-to-update-adguard-home-manually"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#manual-update" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>In case the button isn't shown or an automatic update has failed, you can
update manually.  In the examples below, we'll use AdGuard Home releases for
Linux and Windows for AMD64 CPUs.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element"><a href="#manual-update-unix" id="user-content-manual-update-unix" name="user-content-manual-update-unix">Unix (Linux, macOS, BSD)</a></h3><a id="user-content-unix-linux-macos-bsd" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Unix (Linux, macOS, BSD)" href="#unix-linux-macos-bsd"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#manual-update-unix" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Download the new AdGuard Home package from the <a href="https://github.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/releases/latest">releases page</a>.
If you want to perform this step from the command line:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="curl -L -S -o '/tmp/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz' -s\
    'https://static.adguard.com/adguardhome/release/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz'"><pre>curl -L -S -o <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/tmp/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -s\
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://static.adguard.com/adguardhome/release/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<p>Or, with <code>wget</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="wget -O '/tmp/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz'\
    'https://static.adguard.com/adguardhome/release/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz'"><pre>wget -O <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/tmp/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>\
    <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://static.adguard.com/adguardhome/release/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Navigate to the directory where AdGuard Home was installed.  On most Unix
systems the default directory is <code>/opt/AdGuardHome</code>, but on macOS it's
<code>/Applications/AdGuardHome</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Stop AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo ./AdGuardHome -s stop"><pre>sudo ./AdGuardHome -s stop</pre></div>
<p>(On OpenBSD you probably want to use <code>doas</code> instead of <code>sudo</code>.)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Backup your data.  That is, your configuration file and the data directory
(<code>AdGuardHome.yaml</code> and <code>data/</code> by default).  For example, to backup your
data to a new directory called <code>~/my-agh-backup</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="mkdir -p ~/my-agh-backup
cp -r ./AdGuardHome.yaml ./data ~/my-agh-backup/"><pre>mkdir -p <span class="pl-k">~</span>/my-agh-backup
cp -r ./AdGuardHome.yaml ./data <span class="pl-k">~</span>/my-agh-backup/</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Unpack the AdGuard Home archive to a temporary directory.  For example, if
you downloaded the archive to your <code>~/Downloads</code> directory and want to
unpack it to <code>/tmp/</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="tar -C /tmp/ -f ~/Downloads/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz -x -v -z"><pre>tar -C /tmp/ -f <span class="pl-k">~</span>/Downloads/AdGuardHome_linux_amd64.tar.gz -x -v -z</pre></div>
<p>On macOS, something like:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="unzip -d /tmp/ ~/Downloads/AdGuardHome_darwin_amd64.zip"><pre>unzip -d /tmp/ <span class="pl-k">~</span>/Downloads/AdGuardHome_darwin_amd64.zip</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Replace the old AdGuard Home executable file with the new one.  On most Unix
systems the command would look something like:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo cp /tmp/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome /opt/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome"><pre>sudo cp /tmp/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome /opt/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome</pre></div>
<p>On macOS, something like:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo cp /tmp/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome /Applications/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome"><pre>sudo cp /tmp/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome /Applications/AdGuardHome/AdGuardHome</pre></div>
<p>You may also want to copy the documentation parts of the package, such as
the change log (<code>CHANGELOG.md</code>), the README file (<code>README.md</code>), and the
license (<code>LICENSE.txt</code>).</p>
<p>You can now remove the temporary directory.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Restart AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="sudo ./AdGuardHome -s start"><pre>sudo ./AdGuardHome -s start</pre></div>
<p>(On OpenBSD you probably want to use <code>doas</code> instead of <code>sudo</code>.)</p>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element"><a href="#manual-update-win" id="user-content-manual-update-win" name="user-content-manual-update-win">Windows (Using PowerShell)</a></h3><a id="user-content-windows-using-powershell" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Windows (Using PowerShell)" href="#windows-using-powershell"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#manual-update-win" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>In all examples below, the PowerShell must be run as Administrator.</p>
<ol>
<li>
<p>Download the new AdGuard Home package from the <a href="https://github.com/AdguardTeam/AdGuardHome/releases/latest">releases page</a>.
If you want to perform this step from the command line:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$outFile = Join-Path -Path $Env:USERPROFILE -ChildPath 'Downloads\AdGuardHome_windows_amd64.zip'
$aghUri = 'https://static.adguard.com/adguardhome/release/AdGuardHome_windows_amd64.zip'
Invoke-WebRequest -OutFile &quot;$outFile&quot; -Uri &quot;$aghUri&quot;"><pre><span class="pl-smi">$outFile</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Join-Path</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-smi">$<span class="pl-c1">Env:</span>USERPROFILE</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>ChildPath <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Downloads\AdGuardHome_windows_amd64.zip<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-smi">$aghUri</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://static.adguard.com/adguardhome/release/AdGuardHome_windows_amd64.zip<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-c1">Invoke-WebRequest</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>OutFile <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$outFile</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Uri <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$aghUri</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Navigate to the directory where AdGuard Home was installed.  In the examples
below, we'll use <code>C:\Program Files\AdGuardHome</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Stop AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=".\AdGuardHome.exe -s stop"><pre>.\<span class="pl-c1">AdGuardHome.exe</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>s stop</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Backup your data.  That is, your configuration file and the data directory
(<code>AdGuardHome.yaml</code> and <code>data/</code> by default).  For example, to backup your
data to a new directory called <code>my-agh-backup</code>:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$newDir = Join-Path -Path $Env:USERPROFILE -ChildPath 'my-agh-backup'
New-Item -Path $newDir -ItemType Directory
Copy-Item -Path .\AdGuardHome.yaml, .\data -Destination $newDir -Recurse"><pre><span class="pl-smi">$newDir</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Join-Path</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-smi">$<span class="pl-c1">Env:</span>USERPROFILE</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>ChildPath <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>my-agh-backup<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-c1">New-Item</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-smi">$newDir</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>ItemType Directory
<span class="pl-c1">Copy-Item</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path .\AdGuardHome.yaml<span class="pl-k">,</span> .\<span class="pl-k">data</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Destination <span class="pl-smi">$newDir</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Recurse</pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Unpack the AdGuard Home archive to a temporary directory.  For example, if
you downloaded the archive to your <code>Downloads</code> directory and want to
unpack it to a temporary directory:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$outFile = Join-Path -Path $Env:USERPROFILE -ChildPath 'Downloads\AdGuardHome_windows_amd64.zip'
Expand-Archive -Path &quot;$outFile&quot; -DestinationPath $Env:TEMP"><pre><span class="pl-smi">$outFile</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Join-Path</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-smi">$<span class="pl-c1">Env:</span>USERPROFILE</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>ChildPath <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>Downloads\AdGuardHome_windows_amd64.zip<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-c1">Expand-Archive</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$outFile</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>DestinationPath <span class="pl-smi">$<span class="pl-c1">Env:</span>TEMP</span></pre></div>
</li>
<li>
<p>Replace the old AdGuard Home executable file with the new one.  For example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="$aghExe = Join-Path -Path $Env:TEMP -ChildPath 'AdGuardHome\AdGuardHome.exe'
Copy-Item -Path &quot;$aghExe&quot; -Destination .\AdGuardHome.exe"><pre><span class="pl-smi">$aghExe</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Join-Path</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-smi">$<span class="pl-c1">Env:</span>TEMP</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>ChildPath <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>AdGuardHome\AdGuardHome.exe<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
<span class="pl-c1">Copy-Item</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Path <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$aghExe</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>Destination .\<span class="pl-c1">AdGuardHome.exe</span></pre></div>
<p>You may also want to copy the documentation parts of the package, such as
the change log (<code>CHANGELOG.md</code>), the README file (<code>README.md</code>), and the
license (<code>LICENSE.txt</code>).</p>
<p>You can now remove the temporary directory.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Restart AdGuard Home:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-powershell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=".\AdGuardHome.exe -s start"><pre>.\<span class="pl-c1">AdGuardHome.exe</span> <span class="pl-k">-</span>s start</pre></div>
</li>
</ol>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h2 class="heading-element"><a href="#uninstall" id="user-content-uninstall" name="user-content-uninstall">How to uninstall AdGuard Home?</a></h2><a id="user-content-how-to-uninstall-adguard-home" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: How to uninstall AdGuard Home?" href="#how-to-uninstall-adguard-home"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-alert markdown-alert-warning"><p class="markdown-alert-title"><svg class="octicon octicon-alert mr-2" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="M6.457 1.047c.659-1.234 2.427-1.234 3.086 0l6.082 11.378A1.75 1.75 0 0 1 14.082 15H1.918a1.75 1.75 0 0 1-1.543-2.575Zm1.763.707a.25.25 0 0 0-.44 0L1.698 13.132a.25.25 0 0 0 .22.368h12.164a.25.25 0 0 0 .22-.368Zm.53 3.996v2.5a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0v-2.5a.75.75 0 0 1 1.5 0ZM9 11a1 1 0 1 1-2 0 1 1 0 0 1 2 0Z"></path></svg>Warning</p><p>This section is outdated.  See the <a href="https://adguard-dns.io/kb/adguard-home/faq/#uninstall" rel="nofollow">up-to-date version</a> in our Knowledge Base.</p>
</div>
<p>The way to uninstall AdGuard Home depends on how you installed it.</p>
<p><strong>IMPORTANT:</strong> After uninstalling AdGuard Home, don't forget to change your
devices configuration and point them to a different DNS server.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Regular installation</h3><a id="user-content-regular-installation" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Regular installation" href="#regular-installation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>In this case you need to do the following:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Unregister AdGuard Home service: <code>./AdGuardHome -s uninstall</code>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Remove the AdGuard Home directory.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Docker</h3><a id="user-content-docker" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Docker" href="#docker"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p>Simply stop and remove the image.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading"><h3 class="heading-element">Snap Store</h3><a id="user-content-snap-store" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Snap Store" href="#snap-store"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="snap remove adguard-home"><pre>snap remove adguard-home</pre></div>

              </div>

          </div>
</div>
  <div style="min-width: 0" data-view-component="true" class="Layout-sidebar">          <div class="wiki-rightbar">

<div class="Box Box--condensed color-shadow-small">
